AI summary (Gemini 2.5 Pro) · 20260512T191113Z

Overall

This report for the `so_extraction` agent shows that while all 3,570 runs completed successfully, the quality of the output varies significantly depending on the model used. The overall field match rate is ~81%, with an average of 4.5 mismatched fields per run. However, the provided leaderboard is truncated and only displays the 50 worst-performing model/few-shot combinations. Based on this limited data, `sonnet-4-6` is the best model, while the Gemini models and `openai:5-mini` are the worst. The impact of few-shot examples appears to be minimal.

What the numbers mean

Success Rate: The percentage of runs that completed without an agent or HTTP error. Here, it's 100%, indicating system reliability but not output quality. Avg Runtime: The average wall time in seconds for a combination to complete. Avg Mismatch/Expected Run: The average number of fields in the agent's JSON output that differed from the golden reference JSON. Lower is better. Field Match Rate: The percentage of total fields that correctly matched the golden reference JSON across all runs for a given combination. Higher is better. Mismatch Stdev: The population standard deviation of mismatch counts across all 3570 individual runs. The high value here (~5.13) indicates large variability in quality from one run to the next.

Leaderboard highlights

The provided leaderboard is truncated, showing only the 50 worst-performing combinations out of 70 total. Within this view, `sonnet-4-6` with 0 few-shots is the strongest performer, achieving the highest field match rate (~87%). The weakest models are clearly `gemini:gemini-2.5-flash`, `gemini:gemini-2.5-pro`, and `openai:5-mini`, which have the lowest field match rates (74-76%). For most models shown, varying the few-shot count (`fs_count`) has a minimal or inconsistent impact on quality. Notably, the older `openai:4.1` model (field match rate ~84%) significantly outperforms the newer `openai:5.x` series models shown in this brief. In terms of speed, `openai:4.1` is the fastest at ~1.6s, while `openai:5-mini` is the slowest at ~30s.

What looks healthy

  • The harness and agent are operationally stable, with a 100% success rate across 3,570 runs.
  • The `sonnet-4-6` model with 0 few-shots is the top performer within this truncated leaderboard, achieving an ~87% field match rate.
  • The `openai:4.1` model provides a strong combination of speed (~1.6s) and quality (~84% field match rate).

What needs attention

  • The `gemini` models (`gemini-2.5-pro` and `gemini-2.5-flash`) and `openai:5-mini` perform poorly, with the highest rates of field mismatch.
  • The newer `openai:5.x` models in this list show a lower extraction quality than the older `openai:4.1` model.
  • The number of few-shot examples (`fs_count`) does not appear to be a significant lever for improving performance for the models shown.
  • There is high variance in quality across individual runs (mismatch stdev of 5.13), suggesting inconsistent performance.
